## MANDATORY: Use Sourcegraph MCP Tools

You have Sourcegraph MCP tools available for this task. Using these tools is a **required part of solving this task** — not optional.

### REQUIRED: Use Deep Search (`mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch`)

You have access to **Deep Search** — a powerful semantic code analysis tool. You **MUST** use it as your **first action** when starting this task, before any other exploration.

**Step 0 (BEFORE everything else):** Run `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch` with a query describing what this task requires. For example:
- "How does [feature/component from the task] work in this codebase?"
- "Where is [concept from the task] implemented and what are its dependencies?"
- "Trace the code path for [operation described in the task]"

Deep Search understands code semantically — it traces call chains, data flows, and architectural relationships across files. It is **far more effective** than keyword search for understanding how code fits together.

**When to use Deep Search (mandatory for all of these):**
- Understanding how a feature or subsystem works end-to-end
- Tracing data flow or request lifecycle across multiple files
- Finding all the places that need to change for a cross-cutting modification
- Understanding architectural relationships before making changes
- Any time you need to understand "how does X work?" or "what calls Y?"

**Use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch_read`** to retrieve the full content of any Deep Search result.

Do NOT skip Deep Search and jump straight to keyword search or file browsing. Deep Search gives you the architectural context you need to solve the task correctly.


### Step 1 (REQUIRED before any code changes):
Before you read, edit, or write ANY code, you MUST first use Sourcegraph MCP to explore the codebase:
1. Use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_list_files` to understand the project structure
2. Use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_keyword_search` to locate the relevant code for this task
3. Use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_read_file` to read key files through Sourcegraph

Repository filter for sg_keyword_search: `repo:^github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest$ QUERY`

### Step 2: Continue using MCP throughout
- Instead of Grep -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_keyword_search`
- Instead of Glob -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_list_files`
- For symbol definitions -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_go_to_definition`
- For all references -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_find_references`
- For complex code understanding questions, use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch`

If you catch yourself reaching for Grep or Glob to *find* code, STOP and use Sourcegraph instead.
The only acceptable use of Grep/Glob is verifying content in a file you already located via Sourcegraph.

# Add New API Endpoint to Copilot Arena Server

**Repository:** copilot-arena-server (TheAgentCompany GitLab)  
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM  
**Category:** ccb_tac  
**Task Type:** API Development

## Description

Clone an API server codebase, understand the existing endpoint implementation patterns,
and add a new mock endpoint that mirrors an existing endpoint's response format.

**Why this benefits from MCP:**
- Understanding existing endpoint implementation patterns
- Finding how the `create_pair` endpoint works
- Understanding the API structure and return formats
- Navigating the codebase to find relevant files

## Task

1. Find copilot arena's API server codebase in GitLab 
   (http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/copilot-arena-server)
2. Clone the server repository to the /workspace folder
3. Start up the API server locally
4. Install the correct requirements by running `pip install -r requirements.txt`
5. Create a new POST endpoint to the server called `mock_create_pair`
6. It should return the same JSON as `create_pair`, except with "test" as both 
   the completions, rather than actually calling any APIs
7. Start the server in the background using:
   ```
   uvicorn app:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 5000 --workers 1 --log-config log_conf.yaml
   ```

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully  
[x] Server running on port 5000  
[x] mock_create_pair endpoint returns expected JSON format  
[x] Completions in response are "test" strings

## Notes

- This task tests understanding of existing API patterns
- MCP helps quickly understand the create_pair implementation
- Deterministic grading via API response validation

     1→import yaml
     2→import base64
     3→import os
     4→from typing import List, Dict
     5→from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
     6→
     7→
     8→def get_settings():
     9→    config_path = "config/app_config.yaml"
    10→    if os.path.exists(config_path):
    11→        with open(config_path, "r") as file:
    12→            return yaml.safe_load(file)
    13→
    14→    # Fall back to environment variable
    15→
    16→    load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
    17→    encoded_config = os.getenv("APP_CONFIG_YAML")
    18→    print("encoded config")
    19→    print(encoded_config)
    20→
    21→    # Decode base64 encoded YAML
    22→    try:
    23→        yaml_content = base64.b64decode(encoded_config).decode("utf-8")
    24→        return yaml.safe_load(yaml_content)
    25→    except Exception as e:
    26→        raise ValueError(f"Failed to decode configuration: {str(e)}")
    27→
    28→
    29→def get_models_by_tags(tags: List, models: List, tag_to_models: Dict):
    30→    if not tags or len(tags) == 0:
    31→        return models
    32→    tagged_models = set()
    33→    for tag in tags:
    34→        tagged_models.update(tag_to_models.get(tag, set()))
    35→    return list(tagged_models)
    36→
    37→
    38→def get_cost(prompt_token_length: int, response_token_length: int, model: str):
    39→    config = get_settings()
    40→    model_config = config["models"][model]
    41→    return (
    42→        prompt_token_length * model_config["input_cost"]
    43→        + response_token_length * model_config["output_cost"]
    44→    ) / 1000000
    45→

     1→import pandas as pd
     2→from google.cloud import storage
     3→import logging
     4→import io

     6→logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
     7→
     8→
     9→class GCPClient:
    10→    def __init__(
    11→        self,
    12→        project_id: str = "code-arena",
    13→        credentials_path: str = "config/firebase_config.json",
    14→    ):
    15→        """
    16→        Initialize GCP client with project and credentials.
    17→
    18→        Args:
    19→            project_id: The Google Cloud project ID
    20→            credentials_path: Path to the service account credentials JSON file
    21→        """
    22→        self.storage_client = storage.Client.from_service_account_json(
    23→            credentials_path, project=project_id
    24→        )
    25→
    26→    def get_outcomes_df(self, bucket_name: str, file_path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    27→        """
    28→        Retrieve and parse the outcomes DataFrame from Google Cloud Storage.
    29→
    30→        Args:
    31→            bucket_name: Name of the GCS bucket
    32→            file_path: Path to the CSV file within the bucket
    33→
    34→        Returns:
    35→            pandas.DataFrame containing the outcomes data
    36→        """
    37→        try:
    38→            logger.info(f"Fetching outcomes data from gs://{bucket_name}/{file_path}")
    39→
    40→            # Get bucket and blob
    41→            bucket = self.storage_client.bucket(bucket_name)
    42→            blob = bucket.blob(file_path)
    43→
    44→            # Download the content as string
    45→            content = blob.download_as_string()
    46→
    47→            # Parse CSV content into DataFrame
    48→            df = pd.read_csv(io.BytesIO(content))
    49→

Uploads to Firebase and tracks in Amplitude\n\n### External API Calls\n\nThe endpoint makes the following external API calls:\n\n**1. LLM Provider APIs** (via `timed_create()` in [L86-109](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/blob/server/app.py?L86-L109))\n   - Calls `client.create()` on two different model clients concurrently\n   - Supported providers (from [server/apis/](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/tree/server/apis)):\n     - OpenAI (`openai_client.py`)\n     - Anthropic (`anthropic_client.py`)\n     - Google Gemini (`gemini_client.py`)\n     - Mistral (`mistral_client.py`)\n     - Fireworks (`fireworks_client.py`)\n     - DeepSeek (`deepseek_client.py`, `deepseek_fim_client.py`)\n     - Mercury Coder (`mercury_coder.py`)\n\n**2. Amplitude Analytics** (background tasks)\n   - `create_pair` event - Tracked immediately ([L792-795](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/blob/server/app.py?L792-L795))\n   - `create_pair_success` event - Tracked with model metadata and costs ([L1002-1017](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/blob/server/app.py?L1002-L1017))\n\n**3. Firebase Firestore** (background tasks)\n   - Uploads both completion items to the `all_completions` collection ([L1018-1030](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/blob/server/app.py?L1018-L1030))\n\n### Rate Limiting\n\nThe endpoint has a rate limit of **300 requests per minute** ([L732](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-benchmarks/copilot-arena--latest/-/blob/server/app.py?L732)).\n\n## Sources\n\n- Initialize empty DataFrame if fetch fails\n            self.global_outcomes_df = pd.DataFrame()\n\n    def add_client(self, client: IBaseClient):\n        for model in client.models:\n            if model in self.settings[\"models\"]:\n                self.model_clients[model] = client\n                for tag in self.settings[\"models\"][model][\"tags\"]:\n                    if tag not in self.tag_to_models:\n                        self.tag_to_models[tag] = set()\n                    self.tag_to_models[tag].add(model)\n\n        self.models = list(self.model_clients.keys())\n\n    def select_models(self, tags):\n        # Determine if this is an edit request\n        is_edit = \"edit\" in tags\n        dist_key = \"edit\" if is_edit else \"autocomplete\"\n\n        # Get available models with required tags\n        tagged_models = get_models_by_tags(tags, self.models, self.tag_to_models)\n        if len(tagged_models) == 0:\n            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f\"Error in tagged models\")\n\n        # Get all valid model pairs and their probabilities from the distribution\n        valid_pairs = []\n        probabilities = []\n\n        for pair_str, prob in self.distributions[dist_key].items():\n            model1, model2 = pair_str.split(\"|||\")\n            if model1 in tagged_models and model2 in tagged_models:\n                valid_pairs.append((model1, model2))\n                probabilities.append(prob)\n\n        if not valid_pairs:\n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=500, detail=f\"No valid model pairs found for tags: {tags}\"\n            )\n\n        # Normalize probabilities\n        total_prob = sum(probabilities)\n        if total_prob == 0:\n            raise HTTPException(\n                status_code=500, detail=\"Distribution probabilities sum to 0\"\n            )\n        normalized_probs = [p / total_prob for p in probabilities]\n\n        # Select a pair based on the normalized distribution\n        selected_pair = valid_pairs[\n            np.random.choice(len(valid_pairs), p=normalized_probs)\n        ]\n\n        # Randomly shuffle the order\n        if np.random.random() < 0.5:\n            selected_pair = selected_pair[::-1]\n\n        # Get the clients for the selected models\n        client1: IBaseClient = self.model_clients.get(selected_pair[0])\n        client2: IBaseClient = self.model_clients.get(selected_pair[1])\n\n        return list(selected_pair), client1, client2\n\n    def setup_routes(self):\n        @self.app.post(\"/create_edit_pair\")\n        @self.limiter.limit(\"300/minute\")\n        @handle_exceptions(self)\n        async def create_edit_pair(request: Request, background_tasks: BackgroundTasks):\n            start_time = time.time()\n            latency_breakdown = {}\n\n            # import PrivacySetting, clean_data\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\n\nclass FirebaseClient:\n    def __init__(self):\n        firebase_config_path = \"config/firebase_config.json\"\n        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):\n            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)\n        else:\n            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())\n            encoded_key = os.getenv(\"FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY\")\n            config_dict = json.loads(base64.b64decode(encoded_key).decode(\"utf-8\"))\n            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(config_dict)\n        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)\n        self.db = firestore.client()\n        self.call_timestamps = {}\n        self.function_call_count = {\n            \"upload_data\": 0,\n            \"get_autocomplete_outcomes\": 0,\n            \"get_autocomplete_outcomes_count\": 0,\n        }\n\n    def upload_data(self, collection_name: str, data: dict, privacy: PrivacySetting):\n        self.function_call_count[\"upload_data\"] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n        collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        if privacy != PrivacySetting.RESEARCH:\n            data = clean_data(data)\n        collection_ref.add(data)\n\n    def get_autocomplete_outcomes(\n        self, collection_name: str, user_id: str = None, batch_size: int = 1000\n    ):\n        self.function_call_count[\"get_autocomplete_outcomes\"] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n        if user_id and not self._can_make_call(user_id):\n            raise Exception(f\"Rate limit exceeded for user_id: {user_id}\")\n\n        query = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        if user_id:\n            query = query.where(filter=firestore.FieldFilter(\"userId\", \"==\", user_id))\n        dfs = []\n        last_doc = None\n        while True:\n            current_query = query.limit(batch_size)\n            if last_doc:\n                current_query = current_query.start_after(last_doc)\n            outcomes = current_query.get()\n            if not outcomes:\n                break\n            df_batch = pd.DataFrame([x.to_dict() for x in outcomes])\n            dfs.append(df_batch)\n            last_doc = outcomes[-1]\n        if dfs:\n            outcomes_df = pd.concat(dfs, ignore_index=True)\n        else:\n            outcomes_df = pd.DataFrame()\n        if user_id:\n            self._update_call_timestamp(user_id)\n\n        return outcomes_df\n\n    def get_autocomplete_outcomes_count(self, collection_name: str, user_id):\n        self.function_call_count[\"get_autocomplete_outcomes_count\"] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n\n        query = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        if user_id:\n            query = query.where(filter=firestore.FieldFilter(\"userId\", \"==\", user_id))\n\n        aggregate_query = aggregation.AggregationQuery(query)\n        aggregate_query.count(alias=\"all\")\n\n        results = aggregate_query.get()\n        count = results[0][0].value\n\n        if user_id:\n            self._update_call_timestamp(user_id)\n\n        return count\n\n    def _can_make_call(self, user_id: str) -> bool:\n        if user_id not in self.call_timestamps:\n            return True\n        last_call_time = self.call_timestamps[user_id]\n        return datetime.now() - last_call_time > timedelta(seconds=1)\n\n    def _update_call_timestamp(self, user_id: str):\n        self.call_timestamps[user_id] = datetime.now()\n",

Constants for database keys\n    USER_ID_KEY = \"userId\"\n    USERNAME_KEY = \"username\"\n    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = \"passwordHash\"\n    METADATA_KEY = \"metadata\"\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.db = firestore.client()\n        collection_name = \"users\"\n        self.collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)\n        self.function_call_count = {\n            \"get_user_by_id\": 0,\n            \"get_user_by_username\": 0,\n            \"authenticate\": 0,\n            \"create_user\": 0,\n            \"update_user\": 0,\n            \"delete_user\": 0,\n        }\n\n    def track_function_call(self, function_name):\n        self.function_call_count[function_name] += 1\n        print(self.function_call_count)\n\n    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_id\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, \"==\", user_id)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def get_user_by_username(self, username: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"get_user_by_username\")\n        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username)\n        results = query.get()\n        if not results:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        return results[0].to_dict()\n\n    def authenticate(self, username: str, user_id: str, password: str = None):\n        self.track_function_call(\"authenticate\")\n        try:\n            user = self.get_user_by_id(user_id)\n        except:\n            user = self.get_user_by_username(username)\n\n        if self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY not in user.keys():\n            return user\n\n        if password is None:\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n\n        # Decode the base64 string back to bytes\n        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])\n        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), stored_hash):\n            raise PasswordIncorrectError(\"Invalid username or password\")\n        return user\n\n    def create_user(\n        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"create_user\")\n        try:\n            self.get_user_by_username(username)\n            raise UsernameExistsError(\"Username already exists\")\n        except UserNotFoundError:\n            pass\n        user_data = {\n            self.USER_ID_KEY: user_id,\n            self.USERNAME_KEY: username,\n        }\n        if password is not None:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt())\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            user_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(password_hash).decode(\n                \"utf-8\"\n            )\n        if metadata is not None:\n            user_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.add(user_data)\n\n    def update_user(\n        self,\n        username: str = None,\n        old_password: str = None,\n        new_password: str = None,\n        metadata: dict = None,\n    ):\n        self.track_function_call(\"update_user\")\n        user_doc = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, \"==\", username).get()\n        if not user_doc:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with username {username} not found\")\n        doc_id = user_doc[0].id\n        update_data = {}\n        self.authenticate(username, old_password)\n        if new_password:\n            password_hash = bcrypt.hashpw(\n                new_password.encode(\"utf-8\"), bcrypt.gensalt()\n            )\n            # Convert byte string to base64-encoded string\n            update_data[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY] = base64.b64encode(\n                password_hash\n            ).decode(\"utf-8\")\n        if metadata:\n            update_data[self.METADATA_KEY] = metadata\n        self.collection_ref.document(doc_id).update(update_data)\n\n    def delete_user(self, user_id: str):\n        self.track_function_call(\"delete_user\")\n        doc_ref = self.collection_ref.document(user_id)\n        if not doc_ref.get().exists:\n            raise UserNotFoundError(f\"User with ID {user_id} not found\")\n        doc_ref.delete()\n",

5. EDIT /workspace/copilot-arena-server/server/src/firebase_client.py
Before
import os
import base64
import json
import firebase_admin
from firebase_admin import credentials, firestore
from google.cloud.firestore_v1 import aggregation
from src.privacy import PrivacySetting, clean_data
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime, timedelta


class FirebaseClient:
    def __init__(self):
        firebase_config_path = "config/firebase_config.json"
        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)
        else:
            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
            encoded_key = os.getenv("FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
            config_dict = json.loads(base64.b64decode(encoded_key).decode("utf-8"))
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(config_dict)
        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)
        self.db = firestore.client()
        self.call_timestamps = {}
        self.function_call_count = {
            "upload_data": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes_count": 0,
        }
After
import os
import base64
import json
import firebase_admin
from firebase_admin import credentials, firestore
from google.cloud.firestore_v1 import aggregation
from src.privacy import PrivacySetting, clean_data
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime, timedelta


class FirebaseClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.mock_mode = os.getenv("MOCK_FIREBASE", "false").lower() == "true"
        self.db = None
        self.call_timestamps = {}
        self.function_call_count = {
            "upload_data": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes_count": 0,
        }

        if self.mock_mode:
            print("FirebaseClient running in MOCK mode - no real Firebase operations")
            return

        firebase_config_path = "config/firebase_config.json"
        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)
        else:
            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
            encoded_key = os.getenv("FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY")

        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)

After
import os
import base64
import json
import firebase_admin
from firebase_admin import credentials, firestore
from google.cloud.firestore_v1 import aggregation
from src.privacy import PrivacySetting, clean_data
from dotenv import load_dotenv, find_dotenv
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime, timedelta


class FirebaseClient:
    def __init__(self):
        self.mock_mode = os.getenv("MOCK_FIREBASE", "false").lower() == "true"
        self.db = None
        self.call_timestamps = {}
        self.function_call_count = {
            "upload_data": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes": 0,
            "get_autocomplete_outcomes_count": 0,
        }

        if self.mock_mode:
            print("FirebaseClient running in MOCK mode - no real Firebase operations")
            return

        firebase_config_path = "config/firebase_config.json"
        if os.path.exists(firebase_config_path):
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(firebase_config_path)
        else:
            load_dotenv(find_dotenv())
            encoded_key = os.getenv("FIREBASE_ACCOUNT_KEY")
            config_dict = json.loads(base64.b64decode(encoded_key).decode("utf-8"))
            self.cred = credentials.Certificate(config_dict)
        firebase_admin.initialize_app(self.cred)
        self.db = firestore.client()

8. EDIT /workspace/copilot-arena-server/server/src/firebase_client.py
Before
    def get_autocomplete_outcomes(
        self, collection_name: str, user_id: str = None, batch_size: int = 1000
    ):
        self.function_call_count["get_autocomplete_outcomes"] += 1
        print(self.function_call_count)
        if user_id and not self._can_make_call(user_id):
            raise Exception(f"Rate limit exceeded for user_id: {user_id}")

        query = self.db.collection(collection_name)
        if user_id:
            query = query.where(filter=firestore.FieldFilter("userId", "==", user_id))
        dfs = []
        last_doc = None
        while True:
            current_query = query.limit(batch_size)
            if last_doc:
                current_query = current_query.start_after(last_doc)
            outcomes = current_query.get()
            if not outcomes:
                break
            df_batch = pd.DataFrame([x.to_dict() for x in outcomes])
            dfs.append(df_batch)
            last_doc = outcomes[-1]
        if dfs:
            outcomes_df = pd.concat(dfs, ignore_index=True)
        else:
            outcomes_df = pd.DataFrame()
        if user_id:
            self._update_call_timestamp(user_id)

        return outcomes_df
After
    def get_autocomplete_outcomes(
        self, collection_name: str, user_id: str = None, batch_size: int = 1000
    ):

        query = self.db.collection(collection_name)
        if user_id:
            query = query.where(filter=firestore.FieldFilter("userId", "==", user_id))

        aggregate_query = aggregation.AggregationQuery(query)
        aggregate_query.count(alias="all")

        results = aggregate_query.get()

        if user_id:

        return count

    def get_autocomplete_outcomes_count(self, collection_name: str, user_id):
        self.function_call_count["get_autocomplete_outcomes_count"] += 1
        print(self.function_call_count)
        if self.mock_mode:
            print(f"MOCK: Would get autocomplete outcomes count from {collection_name}")
            return 0

        query = self.db.collection(collection_name)
        if user_id:
            query = query.where(filter=firestore.FieldFilter("userId", "==", user_id))

        aggregate_query = aggregation.AggregationQuery(query)
        aggregate_query.count(alias="all")

        results = aggregate_query.get()
        count = results[0][0].value

        if user_id:
            self._update_call_timestamp(user_id)

        return count

After
import pandas as pd
from google.cloud import storage
import logging
import io
import os

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class GCPClient:
    def __init__(
        self,
        project_id: str = "code-arena",
        credentials_path: str = "config/firebase_config.json",
    ):
        """
        Initialize GCP client with project and credentials.

        Args:
            project_id: The Google Cloud project ID
            credentials_path: Path to the service account credentials JSON file
        """
        self.mock_mode = os.getenv("MOCK_FIREBASE", "false").lower() == "true"
        if self.mock_mode:
            print("GCPClient running in MOCK mode - no real GCP operations")
            self.storage_client = None
            return
        self.storage_client = storage.Client.from_service_account_json(
            credentials_path, project=project_id
        )

import base64
import os
from firebase_admin import firestore
import bcrypt


# Custom Errors
class UserNotFoundError(Exception):
    pass


class PasswordIncorrectError(Exception):
    pass


class UsernameExistsError(Exception):
    pass


class UserRepository:
    # Constants for database keys
    USER_ID_KEY = "userId"
    USERNAME_KEY = "username"
    PASSWORD_HASH_KEY = "passwordHash"
    METADATA_KEY = "metadata"

    def __init__(self):
        self.mock_mode = os.getenv("MOCK_FIREBASE", "false").lower() == "true"
        self.db = None
        self.collection_ref = None
        self.function_call_count = {
            "get_user_by_id": 0,
            "get_user_by_username": 0,
            "authenticate": 0,
            "create_user": 0,
            "update_user": 0,
            "delete_user": 0,
        }

        if self.mock_mode:
            print("UserRepository running in MOCK mode - no real Firebase operations")
            return

        self.db = firestore.client()
        collection_name = "users"
        self.collection_ref = self.db.collection(collection_name)
13. EDIT /workspace/copilot-arena-server/server/src/user_repository.py
Before
    def get_user_by_id(self, user_id: str):
        self.track_function_call("get_user_by_id")
        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USER_ID_KEY, "==", user_id)
        results = query.get()
        if not results:
            raise UserNotFoundError(f"User with ID {user_id} not found")
        return results[0].to_dict()

    def get_user_by_username(self, username: str):
        self.track_function_call("get_user_by_username")
        query = self.collection_ref.where(self.USERNAME_KEY, "==", username)
        results = query.get()
        if not results:
            raise UserNotFoundError(f"User with username {username} not found")
        return results[0].to_dict()

    def authenticate(self, username: str, user_id: str, password: str = None):
        self.track_function_call("authenticate")
        try:
            user = self.get_user_by_id(user_id)
        except:
            user = self.get_user_by_username(username)

        if self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY not in user.keys():
            return user

        if password is None:
            raise PasswordIncorrectError("Invalid username or password")

        # Decode the base64 string back to bytes
        stored_hash = base64.b64decode(user[self.PASSWORD_HASH_KEY])
        if not bcrypt.checkpw(password.encode("utf-8"), stored_hash):
            raise PasswordIncorrectError("Invalid username or password")
        return user

        self, user_id: str, username: str, password: str, metadata: dict = None
    ):

            raise UsernameExistsError("Username already exists")
